      // 웹접근성 적용여부
      function doAcessibility(){
          var enableaccessibility = true;
          var accessibilitytype = "senseleader";
          if (enableaccessibility === undefined) {
              enableaccessibility = application.getPrivateProfile("enableaccessibility", true);
          }
          if (enableaccessibility) {
              if (accessibilitytype === undefined) {
                  accessibilitytype = application.getPrivateProfile("accessibilitytype", true);
              }
          }
          var accessibilityjs = ["./nxc/nexacro14lib/framework/Accessibility.js"];
          application.set_enableaccessibility(enableaccessibility);
          application.set_accessibilitytype(accessibilitytype);
          nexacro.loadJSLibraries(accessibilityjs);
      
      }

      // 쿠키 가져오기
       function getCookie( name ) {
             var nameOfCookie = name + "=";
             var x = 0;
             while ( x <= document.cookie.length )
             {
                 var y = (x+nameOfCookie.length);
                 if ( document.cookie.substring( x, y ) == nameOfCookie ) {
                     if ( (endOfCookie=document.cookie.indexOf( ";", y )) == -1 )
                         endOfCookie = document.cookie.length;
                     return unescape( document.cookie.substring( y, endOfCookie ) );
                 }
                 x = document.cookie.indexOf( " ", x ) + 1;
                 if ( x == 0 )
                     break;
             }
             return "";
          }
      
       function keydowncheck(event)
       {
           var result = true;
           var keycode = "";
      
           if(!event) {
               event= window.event;
               keycode = event.keyCode;
           }
           else { // ff
               keycode = event.which ? event.which : event.keyCode;
           }
      
           if(nexacro.Browser == 'IE') {
               if(123 == keycode) {
                    result = false;
               }
           } else if(nexacro.Browser == 'Chrome') {
               if(123 == keycode
                       || (event.ctrlKey && event.shiftKey && 73 == keycode)
                       || (event.ctrlKey && event.shiftKey && 67 == keycode)
                       || (event.ctrlKey && event.shiftKey && 74 == keycode)
                 )
               {
                    result = false;
               }
           }
           else if(nexacro.Browser == 'Gecko') {
               if(123 == keycode
                       || (event.ctrlKey && event.shiftKey && 73 == keycode)
                       || (event.ctrlKey && event.shiftKey && 75 == keycode)
                       || (event.ctrlKey && event.shiftKey && 83 == keycode)
                       || (event.shiftKey && 118 == keycode)
                       || (event.shiftKey && 116 == keycode)
                       || (event.ctrlKey && event.shiftKey && 81 == keycode)
                 )
               {
                    result = false;
               }
           }
           else if(nexacro.Browser == 'Safari') {
               if((event.ctrlKey && event.altKey && 73 == keycode)
                       || (event.ctrlKey && event.altKey && 67 == keycode)
                       || (event.ctrlKey && event.altKey && 80 == keycode)
                 )
               {
                    result = false;
               }
           }
           return result;
       }
